buy_oil_90 = {
	category = economy
	alert_index = 29
	alert_tooltip = BUY_OIL_90
	require_acceptance = yes # Whether the recipient gets an option to decline
	
	is_visible = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 10
						}
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 10
						}
					}
					check_variable = { which = oil_production value = 70 }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 9
						}
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 9
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 10
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 10
						}
					}
					check_variable = { which = oil_production value = 60 }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						calc_true_if = {

								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 8
						}

							all_owned_province = {

							}
								amount = 9

					}
					check_variable = { which = oil_production value = 50 }

							}
								amount = 7
						}

								trade_goods = electronics

					}
					NOT = {

				}
			}
		}
		
		treasury = 15000
	}
	on_accept = {
		remove_country_modifier = show_oil_modifire
		remove_country_modifier = buy_6milion_oil
		change_variable = { which = bought_oil value = 60 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = bought_oil_1
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_treasury = -15000

			change_variable = { which = oil_sold value = 60 }

			who = ROOT
			modifier = buy_oil_opinion_60
		}
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = ROOT
			modifier = buy_oil_opinion_60
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	on_accept = {
		remove_country_modifier = show_oil_modifire
		remove_country_modifier = buy_9milion_oil
		change_variable = { which = bought_oil value = 50 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = bought_oil_1
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_treasury = -12500
		FROM = { add_treasury = 12500 }
		FROM = { 
			change_variable = { which = oil_sold value = 50 } 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = oil_sold_modifire_50
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = set_variable.39 days = 2  }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion_50
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion_50
			}
		}
		
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
		
		add_entry = {
			name = BASE_EMMBASY
			limit = { always = yes }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 5
			}
		}
					
		add_entry = {
			name = FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_friendly } } }
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 5
				}
	
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = WE_HAVE_GOOD_OPINON_150
			limit = { FROM = { has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 150 }   } }

				name = ALLY_WITH

					value = 15

		}
		add_entry = {

		add_entry = {
			name = YOU_WANT_OUR_LAND
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_hostile } } }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 40
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}

						alliance_with = ROOT

	on_accept = {
		remove_country_modifier = show_oil_modifire
		remove_country_modifier = buy_4milion_oil
		change_variable = { which = bought_oil value = 40 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = bought_oil_1
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_treasury = -10000
		FROM = { add_treasury = 10000 }
		FROM = { 
			change_variable = { which = oil_sold value = 40 } 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = oil_sold_modifire_40
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = set_variable.39 days = 2  }
		add_opinion = {
			who = ROOT
			modifier = buy_oil_opinion_40
		}
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = ROOT
			modifier = buy_oil_opinion_40
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
		
		add_entry = {
			name = BASE_EMMBASY
			limit = { always = yes }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 5
			}
		}
					
		add_entry = {
			name = FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_friendly } } }
				export_to_variable = {

				}

			name = RIVAL_WITH

				}

		}
		add_entry = {
			name = WE_HAVE_BAD_OPINON_100
			limit = { NOT = { FROM = { has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -100 } } } }
			export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value

			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }

		add_entry = {

			limit = { 
				FROM = {
					any_rival_country = {
						alliance_with = ROOT
					}

					value = 30
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
	
		}

	}

buy_oil_30 = {
	category = economy
	alert_index = 29
	alert_tooltip = BUY_OIL_30
	require_acceptance = yes # Whether the recipient gets an option to decline
	
	is_visible = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 10
						}
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 10
						}
					}
					check_variable = { which = oil_production value = 70 }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 9
						}
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 9
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 10
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 10
						}
					}
					check_variable = { which = oil_production value = 60 }
				}

	category = economy

					check_variable = {

	on_accept = {
		remove_country_modifier = show_oil_modifire
		remove_country_modifier = buy_0_8milion_oil
		change_variable = { which = bought_oil value = 8 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = bought_oil_1
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_treasury = -2000
		FROM = { add_treasury = 2000 }
		FROM = { 
			change_variable = { which = oil_sold value = 8 } 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = oil_sold_modifire_8
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = set_variable.39 days = 2  }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
		
		add_entry = {
			name = BASE_EMMBASY
			limit = { always = yes }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 5
			}
		}
					
		add_entry = {
			name = FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_friendly } } }

	on_accept = {
		remove_country_modifier = show_oil_modifire
		remove_country_modifier = buy_0_7milion_oil
		change_variable = { which = bought_oil value = 7 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = bought_oil_1
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_treasury = -1750
		FROM = { add_treasury = 1750 }
		FROM = { 
			change_variable = { which = oil_sold value = 7 } 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = oil_sold_modifire_7
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = set_variable.39 days = 2  }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
		
		add_entry = {
			name = BASE_EMMBASY
			limit = { always = yes }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 5
			}
		}
					
		add_entry = {
			name = FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_friendly } } }
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 5
				}
	
		}

					value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
	
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = WE_HAVE_BAD_OPINON_25
			limit = { NOT = { FROM = { has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -25 } } } }
			export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
	
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = MY_RIVAL_ALIIY_WITH_YOU
			limit = { 
				FROM = {
					any_rival_country = {
						alliance_with = ROOT
					}
				}				
			} 
			export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 30
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
	
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes
	}

buy_oil_05 = {
	category = economy
	alert_index = 29
	alert_tooltip = BUY_OIL_05
	require_acceptance = yes # Whether the recipient gets an option to decline
	
	is_visible = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 10
						}
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 10
						}
					}
					check_variable = { which = oil_production value = 70 }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 9
						}
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 9
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 10
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 10
						}
					}
					check_variable = { which = oil_production value = 60 }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 8
						}
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 8
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 9
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 9
						}
					}
					check_variable = { which = oil_production value = 50 }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = cars
							}
								amount = 7
						}
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								trade_goods = electronics
							}
								amount = 7
						}
					}
					NOT = {

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = oil_production
						value = 3
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = { 
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = oil_sold
						value = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = oil_production
						value = 2
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = { 
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = oil_sold
						value = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = { 
				check_variable = {
					which = oil_production
					value = 1
				}
			}
			FROM = { 
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = oil_sold
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		treasury = 500
	}
	on_accept = {
		remove_country_modifier = show_oil_modifire
		remove_country_modifier = buy_0_2milion_oil
		change_variable = { which = bought_oil value = 2 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = bought_oil_1
			duration = 3650
		}
		change_variable = { which = bought_oil value = 2 }
		add_treasury = -500
		FROM = { add_treasury = 500 }
		FROM = { 
			change_variable = { which = oil_sold value = 2 } 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = oil_sold_modifire_2
				duration = 1825
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

					any_rival_country = {

					value = 30

			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
	
		}

	on_accept = {
		remove_country_modifier = show_oil_modifire
		remove_country_modifier = buy_0_1milion_oil
		change_variable = { which = bought_oil value = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = bought_oil_1
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_treasury = -250
		FROM = { add_treasury = 250 }
		FROM = { 
			change_variable = { which = oil_sold value = 1 } 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = oil_sold_modifire_1
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = set_variable.39 days = 2  }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = buy_oil_opinion
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
		
		add_entry = {
			name = BASE_EMMBASY
			limit = { always = yes }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 5
			}
		}
					
		add_entry = {
			name = FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_friendly } } }
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 5
				}
	
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = WE_HAVE_GOOD_OPINON_150
			limit = { FROM = { has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 150 }   } }
			export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 15

		}
		add_entry = {

		}
		add_entry = {
				name = OPINION
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value
					value = opinion
					who = FROM
					with = THIS
				}
				divide_variable = { which = ai_value value = 5 }
			}
		
		add_entry = {
				name = ALLY_WITH
				limit = { FROM = { alliance_with = ROOT } } 
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 15
				}
		
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_friendly } } }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 25
			}
			
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_threatened } } }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 15
			}
			
		}
		
		add_entry = {
			name = YOU_WANT_OUR_LAND
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_hostile } } }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 40
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = RIVAL_WITH
			limit = { FROM = { ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_rivalry } } }
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value 
				value = 100
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		
		add_entry = {
				name = RIVAL_WITH
				limit = { FROM = { is_rival = ROOT } }
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 100
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = WE_HAVE_BAD_OPINON_100
			limit = { NOT = { FROM = { has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -100 } } } }
			export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 15
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
	
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = WE_HAVE_BAD_OPINON_50
			limit = { NOT = { FROM = { has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -50 } } } }
			export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
	
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = WE_HAVE_BAD_OPINON_25
			limit = { NOT = { FROM = { has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -25 } } } }
			export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
	
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = MY_RIVAL_ALIIY_WITH_YOU
			limit = { 
				FROM = {
					any_rival_country = {
						alliance_with = ROOT
					}
				}				
			} 
			export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = ai_value 
					value = 30
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
	
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes
	}
